var randingBnGI = new Array();
var randingBnGG = new Array();
var bnnr_no;

randingBnGI[0] = {"background":"#fee250", "target":"_blank", "src":"http://file3.jobkorea.co.kr/albamon/notice/Mon_20150818.jpg", "alt":"기업회원 감사 이벤트 알바생도 구하시고 100% 당첨선물까지 받는 1석2조 이벤트", "url":"/event/2015corpthanks/","bnnr_no":"43"}


if( randingBnMain.length > 0 ) {
	var randingBnNum=Math.floor(Math.random() * (randingBnMain.length));
	$("#dev_landingBn").css("background", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].background);
	$("#dev_landingBn a").attr("href", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].url);
	$("#dev_landingBn a").attr("target", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].target);
	$("#dev_landingBn a>img").attr("src", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].src);
	$("#dev_landingBn a>img").attr("alt", randingBnMain[randingBnNum].alt);
	bnnr_no = randingBnMain[randingBnNum].bnnr_no;
}


function landingBnClickCnt() {
	albamontargetURL.location.href  = "/etc/gnbtopbn_cnt.asp?bnnr_no="+bnnr_no;
}

$(function(){
	
	if( randingBnMain.length > 0 ) {
		var randingBnCookie = getCookie("dev_randingBnMain20131015");
		if(randingBnCookie != null){
			$("#dev_landingBn").hide();
		}
		else {
			$("#dev_landingBn").slideDown(400, function(){  
				$("#div_fly_right").css('top','300px');
			});

			$("#dev_landingBn button").click(function() {
				var nowDate = new Date();
				var nowHours = nowDate.getHours();
				var nowMinutes = nowDate.getMinutes();
				var cookie_time =  (60*(24*7)) - (nowHours*60 + nowMinutes); // 7일
				setCookie('dev_randingBnMain20131015', 'yes', cookie_time, '/', 'albamon.com');
				$("#dev_landingBn").hide();
			});
		}
	}
	
});
</script>

			<script type="text/javascript">
			//<![CDATA[
			var ch = false;
			function change() {
				if ( ch ) return;
				document.frmsubkey.Key_Word.value="";
				//document.frmsubkey.Key_Word.style.backgroundImage="";
				ch = true;
			}

			function subkey_send() {
				var kwd =  document.frmsubkey.Key_Word.value;
				var smgubun =  document.frmsubkey.smgubun.value;
				kwd = kwd.replace(/"/gi, "");

				if(kwd == "") {
					alert("키워드를 입력하세요");
					document.frmsubkey.Key_Word.value="";
					document.frmsubkey.Key_Word.focus();
					return false;
				}
				kwd = go_replace_text(kwd);
				var url = "smtext=" + kwd+"&smgubun="+smgubun;
				url = "/sm/sm_syn_list.asp?"+url+"&searchkey=1" ;
				top.location.href = url;
				return false;

			}

			//검색키 변환
			function go_replace_text(stext) {
				for(var i=0; i < stext.length;i++){
					if(stext.indexOf("+") != -1){
						 stext=stext.replace("+","%2B")
					}
					if(stext.indexOf("#") != -1){
						 stext=stext.replace("#","%23")
					}
					if(stext.indexOf("&") != -1){
						 stext=stext.replace("&","%26")
					}
				}
				return stext;
			}
			//]]>
			</script>

				$(document).ready(function() {
					$("ul.gMenu > li:not(.navLi.fr)").each(function(index, ele) { //신입공채 제외
						var ele =  $(this);
						ele.hover(function() { $(" > div", ele).show(); $(" > a", ele).addClass("on"); }
								,	function() { $(" > div", ele).hide(); $(" > a", ele).removeClass("on"); }
						);
						ele.focusin(function() {
							$("ul.gMenu > li").not(this).each(function(){
								if( $(this).css("display") != "none" ) { $(" > div", this).hide(); $(" > a", this).removeClass("on");}
							});
							$(" > div", ele).show();  $(" > a", ele).addClass("on");
						});

						$(" > div .btnClose", ele).click(function(){ $(" > div", ele).hide(); $(" > a", ele).removeClass("on"); });
						$(" > div .btnClose", ele).focusout(function(){ $(" > div", ele).hide(); $(" > a", ele).removeClass("on"); });
					});

					
					//공고등록
					{
						var ele1 = $("ul.subNav > li").eq(1);
						ele1.hover(function() { $(" > div.layerAn",  $(this)).show(); $(" > a",  $(this)).addClass("on"); }
									,	function() { $(" > div.layerAn",  $(this)).hide(); $(" > a",  $(this)).removeClass("on"); }
						);
						ele1.focusin(function() { $(" > div.layerAn",  $(this)).show();  $(" > a",  $(this)).addClass("on");});
						$(" > div .btnClose", ele1).click(function(){ $(" > div.layerAn", ele1).hide(); $(" > a", ele1).removeClass("on"); });
						$(" > div .btnClose", ele1).focusout(function(){ $(" > div.layerAn", ele1).hide(); $(" > a", ele1).removeClass("on"); });

						$("ul.subNav > li").eq(0).focusin(function() {
							if( $("div.layerAn").css("display") != "none" ) { $("div.layerAn").hide(); $(" > a", $("ul.subNav > li").eq(1)).removeClass("on"); }
						});

					}
					
				});
			
			</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function gnbiBinit(t,obj){	
	var gnbnoticeObj = $('#'+obj+' li');
	gnbnoticeObj.each(function(index) {
		if( index == t) $(this).show();
		else $(this).hide();			
	});	
}
</script>



<script type="text/javascript">		
//gnb 우측 배너
function gnbiBpn2(t,obj){
	var gnbnoticeObj = $('#'+obj+' li');
	var gnbNoticelength = gnbnoticeObj.length;		
	if(t=='n'){gnbiPv2++;if(gnbiPv2 >= gnbNoticelength){gnbiPv2=0;}}
	if(t=='p'){gnbiPv2--;if(gnbiPv2 < 0){gnbiPv2=eval(gnbNoticelength)-1;}}
	gnbiBinit(gnbiPv2,obj);	
}
var gnbiPv2=Math.ceil(Math.random() * $('#dev_gnbNotice2 li').length-1);	
gnbiBinit(gnbiPv2,'dev_gnbNotice2');	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	/*
		로그인 공통 JS 함수
		2013-07-16 장용 생성
	*/
	function SendLogin(){
		try{
			var DBNameVal = $("[name='DB_Name']:radio:checked").val();
			var giHomeUrl = "http://www.albamon.com/corp/mon_gi_home.asp";
			var ggHomeUrl = "http://www.albamon.com/mem/mon_gg_home.asp";

			if($("[name='DB_Name'][type='hidden']:input").length == 0){
				if(DBNameVal == undefined){
					alert("개인회원 또는 기업회원을 선택하세요.");
					$("[name='DB_Name'][value='GG']:radio").focus();
					return false;
				}else{
					var reUrl = $("[name='re_url']:input");
					if($(reUrl).val() =="" || $(reUrl).val() ==giHomeUrl || $(reUrl).val()==ggHomeUrl ){
						if(DBNameVal=="GI"){
							$(reUrl).val( giHomeUrl );
						}else if(DBNameVal=="GG"){
							$(reUrl).val( ggHomeUrl );
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if($("#M_ID").val()=="" || $("#M_ID").val()=="아이디"){
				 alert("아이디를 입력하세요."); 
				 $("#M_ID").focus(); 
				 return false;
			}

			if($("#M_PWD").val()==""){
				alert("비밀번호를 입력하세요."); 
				if($("#M_PWD_default").length > 0){
					$("#M_PWD_default").focus(); 
				}
				else{
					$("#M_PWD").focus(); 
				}
					
				return false;
			}


			if($("#picText").length >0 && ($("#picText").val()=="" ||  $("#picText").val()=="자동입력 방지 문자")){
				alert("자동입력 방지 문자를 입력하세요."); 
				$("#picText").focus(); 
				return false;
			}

			$("#f").attr("action","https://www.albamon.com/login/login.asp");
		}
		catch(e){
			alert("로그인 시도중 오류가 발생 하였습니다. 다시 시도 해주세요.");
			window.location.reload();
		}finally{}

		return true;
	}

	//로그인 페이지 기본 세팅
	function setDefaultLoginFrom(){
		try{
			if($("#login_pop").val() !="Y" ){
				if($("#M_ID").val()=="" || $("#M_ID").val()=="아이디"){
					SetTextStyle("hint",$("#M_ID"));
					$("#M_ID").val("아이디");
					//$("#M_ID").focus();
				}else{
					SetTextStyle("input",$("#M_ID"));
					$("#M_PWD_default").focus();
				}

				$("#M_ID").keydown(function(){
					if(this.value=="아이디"){
						this.value="";
						SetTextStyle("input",this);
					}
				});

				$("#M_ID").blur(function(){
					if(this.value==""){
						SetTextStyle("hint",this);
						this.value="아이디";
					}
				});

				$("#M_ID").click(function(){
					if(this.value=="아이디"){
						SetTextStyle("input",this);
						this.value="";
					}
				});

				$("#M_PWD_default").keydown(function(){
					$("#pwdDefaultLayer").hide();
					$("#pwdInputLayer").show();
					$("#M_PWD").focus();
				});

				$("#M_PWD").blur(function(){
					if(this.value==""){
						$("#pwdInputLayer").hide();
						$("#pwdDefaultLayer").show();
					}
				});

				$("#M_PWD_default").click(function(){
					$("#pwdDefaultLayer").hide();
					$("#pwdInputLayer").show();
					$("#M_PWD").focus();
				});
			}
			if($("#picText").length >0){
				$("#picText").focus(function(){
					if(this.value=="자동입력 방지 문자"){
						SetTextStyle("input",this);
						this.value="";
					}
				});

				$("#picText").blur(function(){
					if(this.value==""){
						SetTextStyle("hint",this);
						this.value="자동입력 방지 문자";
					}
				});
			}

		}
		catch(e){
			alert("페이지로딩중 오류가 발생 하였습니다. 페이지를 다시 로드 합니다.");
			window.location.reload();
		}finally{
		}
	}

	//그림문자 새로고침
	function ReloadCaptcha() {
		var now = new Date();
		var imgURL;
		try{
			imgURL = $("#imgCaptcha").attr("src").split('?')[0] + '?x=' + now.toUTCString()
			$("#imgCaptcha").attr("src",imgURL);
		}
		catch(e){
			alert("새로고침에 실패 하였습니다. 페이지를 다시 로드 합니다.");
			window.location.reload();
		}
	}

	function SetTextStyle(mode, obj, inputType) {
		var imgName="";
		if(inputType=="id") imgName= "bg_login_id.gif";
		else if(inputType=="pwd") imgName= "bg_login_pwd.gif";

		switch (mode.toUpperCase())
		{
			//style="ime-mode:disabled; font-size:12px;color:#9a9a9a;padding:6px 1px 2px 5px;"
			case  "HINT" :
				$(obj).css("ime-mode", "disabled").css("color", "#9a9a9a");
				//$(obj).css("backgroundImage","url(/monimg/main_2010/"+imgName+")").css("background-repeat","no-repeat");
				break;
			case "INPUT" : 
				$(obj).css("ime-mode", "disabled").css("color", "");
				//$(obj).css("backgroundImage","");
				break;
		}
	}

</script>

		<div class="mainLogin">
		
			<!-- 로그인 전 -->
			<script type="text/javascript">
			//<![CDATA[		

			//쿠키값 얻기
			function getCookie_id(name) {
				var nameStr = name + "=" ;
				var nameLen = nameStr.length;
				var cookieLen = document.cookie.length;		//쿠기값이 없을시 기본적으로 45이다.  document.cookie.length >= 45

				//	a로 지정시 : document.cookie ==> lucya=a; ASPSESSIONIDQGQQGLDC=GKDDHCPDJBOBAONCMJLHBCCN
				var i = 0;
				while( i < cookieLen ) {
					var j = i + nameLen;
					if ( document.cookie.substring(i, j) == nameStr ) {
						var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", j); // ;의 위치
						if( end == -1) end = document.cookie.length;
						return unescape( document.cookie.substring(j, end) ); //쿠키값 반환
					}
					i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
					if ( i == 0) {
						break;
					}
				}
			}
			//]]>
			</script>

			//<![CDATA[	
				function GuinInterestMemSave(){
					var cookieFound = false ;
					var nameStr = "InterestGuinOpt=" ;
					var nameLen = nameStr.length;
					var cookieLen = document.cookie.length;
					var Cookievalue = ""
					var i = 0;
					while( i < cookieLen ) {
						var j = i + nameLen;
						if ( document.cookie.substring(i, j) == nameStr ) {
							var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", j); // ;의 위치
							if( end == -1) end = document.cookie.length;
								Cookievalue = unescape( document.cookie.substring(j, end) ); //쿠키값 반환
								cookieFound = true;
						}
						i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
						if ( i == 0) {
							break;
						}
					}
					var HTML = "";
					if (cookieFound && Cookievalue !="") {
						document.getElementById("GuinOptName").value = Cookievalue;
					}else{
						document.getElementById("GuinOptName").value = "";
					}
				}
				GuinInterestMemSave();
			//]]>

	<script type="text/javascript">
	function GIB_Read(Al_GI_No,Win_Type,optgcode) {
		var expurl = "";
		if(optgcode){
			expurl = "&optgf=" + optgcode;
		}
		var url = "/list/gi/mon_gib_read.asp?AL_GI_No=" + Al_GI_No + expurl;
		if(Win_Type == "2"){	//스킨
			url = "/list/gi/mon_gib_read_skin.asp?AL_GI_No=" + Al_GI_No + expurl ;
			window.open(url, "mon_gib_read_skin","width=865,height=700,scrollbars=yes,location=yes");
		} else if(Win_Type == "1"){	//새창
			window.open(url, "","");
		} else {
			top.location.href = url;
		}
	}
	$(function() {
		//채용 간략보기
		var main_simpleview = $(".pgSimpleGI");
		main_simpleview.each( function (i) {
			$(this).click(function(){
				$('.pgSimpleView').remove();
				$('.dev_optinfolayer').remove();
				$('.pgSimpleViewIfr').remove();
				var al_gi_no = $(this).attr("id").substring(14);
				var optgoodcd = $(this).attr("optgcd");
				var exurl = "";
				if(optgoodcd){
					exurl = "?optgf=" + optgoodcd;
				}
				$(this).simpleLayerView(al_gi_no,595,271,'/list/gi/simpleview_gi.asp'+exurl,'','');
				return false;
			});
		});

		//인재간략보기
		var main_simpleviewGG = $(".pgSimpleGG");
		main_simpleviewGG.each( function (i) {
			$(this).click(function(){
				$('.pgSimpleView').remove();
				$('.dev_optinfolayer').remove();
				$('.pgSimpleViewIfr').remove();
				var m_id = $(this).attr("id").substring(14);
				$(this).simpleLayerView(m_id,545,205,'/list/gg/simpleview_gg.asp','','');
				return false;
			});
		});

		//lotte
		$("#dev_opt_platinum li:not(.dev_Franchise_c)").each(function() { 
			$(this).focusin( function() { $("#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c > div").hide(); });
		});
		$("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c").each(function() { 
			var ele = $(this);
			ele
			.hover(
					function() { $("> div", ele).show(); }
				,	function() { $("> div", ele).hide(); } )
			.focusin( function() { 
				$("div#dev_opt_platinum li.dev_Franchise_c").not(this).each(function(){
					$(" > div", this).hide();
				});
				$("> div", ele).show(); 				
				});		
		}) 
		
	});
	</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			$(document).ready(function(){
				//Top으로 가기 버튼 제어
				$('#dev_topBtn').hide();
				$(function(){
					$(window).scroll(function () {
						if ($(this).scrollTop() > 0) $('#dev_topBtn').fadeIn(100);
						else $('#dev_topBtn').fadeOut(200);
						var minTop = $("#footer").offset().top - $("#dev_topBtn").height();
						if(minTop <= $("#dev_topBtn").offset().top ){
							$("#dev_topBtn").css({position:"absolute"}).offset({top:minTop});
						}
						else{
							var bottomHeight =750;
							var winHeight = $(window).height();
							bottomHeight = bottomHeight > winHeight ? winHeight: bottomHeight
							if($(document).scrollTop()+$("#dev_topBtn").height()+bottomHeight < $("#dev_topBtn").offset().top ) $("#dev_topBtn").css({position:"fixed",top:"auto"});
						}
					});
					$('#dev_topBtn a').click(function () {
						$('body,html').animate({scrollTop: 0}, 300);
						return false;
					});
				});
			});
		</script>
